	<article class="m_feature-nightography bk" id="nightography-camera">
		<div class="sticky-wrap">
			<div class="sticky-inner ykOutH" data-minheight-s4="845" data-minheight-s2="660" data-minheight-s1="650">

					<div class="content-wrap">
						<div class="f_container">
							<div class="f_header-type1">
								<h3 class="c_cate-type2">НОЧНОЙ РЕЖИМ</h3>
								<strong class="c_feature-type2">Ночь правит</strong>
								<div class="text-wrap">
									<div class="copy-wrap">
										<p class="c_desc-type1">Ночные кадры еще никогда не были настолько хороши. Инновационный большой пиксельный сенсор обеспечит минимальные шумы даже в самых темных пространствах. А супергладкое стекло линз смягчит блики объектива для четких, ярких кадров.</p>
										<div class="dropdown-wrap">
											<ul role="list">
												<li class="dropdown_item" role="listitem">
													<h4 class="dropdown_item_q">
														<button class="should-scroll" type="button" aria-expanded="false" data-omni-type="microsite_contentinter" data-omni="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:nightography-camera:expand:1" ga-ca="content click" ga-ac="feature" ga-la="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:nightography-camera:expand:1"><em>01</em>Большой Пиксельный Сенсор</button>
													</h4>
													<div class="dropdown_item_a">
														<p>108-мегапиксельная камера с высоким разрешением обладает суперсилой: это наш самый большой пиксельный сенсор. Во время съемки в условиях слабого освещения он объединяет свои пиксели в блоки из девяти пикселей, а полученные пиксели размером 2,4 мкм поглощают много света. Забудьте о зернистости и шумах, теперь только четкие ночные снимки.</p>
													</div>
												</li>
												<li class="dropdown_item" role="listitem">
													<h4 class="dropdown_item_q">
														<button class="should-scroll" type="button" aria-expanded="false" data-omni-type="microsite_contentinter" data-omni="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:nightography-camera:expand:2" ga-ca="content click" ga-ac="feature" ga-la="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:nightography-camera:expand:2"><em>02</em>Сверхпрозрачное стекло и линзы</button>
													</h4>
													<div class="dropdown_item_a">
														<p>Сверхпрозрачное стекло закрывает переднюю часть основной камеры, а широкоугольная камера оснащена суперчеткими линзами — обе линзы имеют эксклюзивное нанопокрытие со сверхнизким коэффициентом отражения. Сверхпрозрачное стекло и линзы помогают уменьшить блики при съемке даже в темноте.</p>
													</div>
												</li>
											</ul>

						<p class="c_desc-type1">Ночной режим - самый большой прорыв в наших видеотехнологиях. Камера оценивает условия освещения и автоматически переключается на оптимальную частоту кадров в секунду. Благодаря 4-нм процессору с Super Night Solution, устраняющему шум в каждом кадре, вы можете записывать от восхода до заката с постоянными потрясающими деталями.</p>

Прежде чем вы нажмете кнопку спуска затвора, Adaptive Pixel переключается между режимом высокого разрешения 108 МП и режимом высокой чувствительности 12 МП, что позволяет получать более яркие и четкие фотографии.<sup>9</sup> Кроме того, он объединяется с интеллектуальным модулем Detail Enhancer для корректировки теней и бликов.</p>

						<p>Galaxy&nbsp;S22 Ultra пишет видео в 8K и позволяет снимать фотографии с разрешением до 33MP с помощью 8K Video Snap.</p>
						<a href="#camera" class="c_btn_f3 btn_big btn_bg_empty" title="" data-omni-type="microsite_contentinter" data-omni="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:faq^2:jump:camera" ga-ca="content click" ga-ac="feature" ga-la="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:faq^2:jump:camera">
							<span class="c_btn_area"><span class="copy">ПЕРЕЙТИ К КАМЕРЕ</span></span>
						</a>
					</div>
				</li>
	
				<li class="faq_item" role="listitem">
					<h3 class="faq_item_q">
						<button type="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq_item1" data-omni-type="microsite_contentinter" data-omni="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:faq^3:expand:3" ga-ca="content click" ga-ac="feature" ga-la="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:faq^3:expand:3">Есть ли у Galaxy&nbsp;S22 Ultra встроенный S&nbsp;Pen?</button>
					</h3>
					<div class="faq_item_a" id="faq_item1">
						<p>Galaxy&nbsp;S22 Ultra — первый смартфон в серии Galaxy S со встроенным пером S&nbsp;Pen. Благодаря точному наконечнику и высокому отклику каждое движение напоминает обычное письмо ручкой. Когда закончите делать заметки, управляйте своим смартфоном с помощью Air Actions с поддержкой Bluetooth. В конце просто поместите перо обратно в телефон для подзарядки.</p>
						<a href="#s-pen" class="c_btn_f3 btn_big btn_bg_empty" title="" data-omni-type="microsite_contentinter" data-omni="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:faq^3:jump:s-pen" ga-ca="content click" ga-ac="feature" ga-la="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:faq^3:jump:s-pen">
							<span class="c_btn_area"><span class="copy">ПЕРЕЙТИ К S&nbsp;PEN</span></span>
						</a>
					</div>
				</li>
	
				<li class="faq_item" role="listitem">
					<h3 class="faq_item_q">
						<button type="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq_item1" data-omni-type="microsite_contentinter" data-omni="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:faq^4:expand:4" ga-ca="content click" ga-ac="feature" ga-la="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:faq^4:expand:4">Есть ли у Galaxy&nbsp;S22 Ultra 100х зум?</button>
					</h3>
					<div class="faq_item_a" id="faq_item1">
						<p>Galaxy&nbsp;S22 Ultra имеет 100-кратный зум благодаря системе двойного телезума с 3-кратным и 10-кратным оптическим зумом и зумом Super Resolution с искусственным интеллектом вплоть до 100-кратного увеличения.</p>
						<a href="#space-zoom" class="c_btn_f3 btn_big btn_bg_empty" title="" data-omni-type="microsite_contentinter" data-omni="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:faq^4:jump:space-zoom" ga-ca="content click" ga-ac="feature" ga-la="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:faq^4:jump:space-zoom">
							<span class="c_btn_area"><span class="copy">ПЕРЕЙТИ К ЗУМУ</span></span>
						</a>
					</div>
				</li>
	
				<li class="faq_item" role="listitem">
					<h3 class="faq_item_q">
						<button type="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq_item1" data-omni-type="microsite_contentinter" data-omni="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:faq^5:expand:5" ga-ca="content click" ga-ac="feature" ga-la="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:faq^5:expand:5">Какой размер экрана у  Galaxy&nbsp;S22 Ultra?</button>
					</h3>
					<div class="faq_item_a" id="faq_item1">
						
						<p>Galaxy&nbsp;S22 Ultra оснащен большим 6,8-дюймовым экраном и кинематографическим соотношением сторон 19,3:9 для полного погружения в просмотр.</p>
						
						
						<a href="#design" class="c_btn_f3 btn_big btn_bg_empty" title="" data-omni-type="microsite_contentinter" data-omni="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:faq^5:jump:design" ga-ca="content click" ga-ac="feature" ga-la="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:faq^5:jump:design">
							<span class="c_btn_area"><span class="copy">ПЕРЕЙТИ К ДИЗАЙНУ</span></span>
						</a>
					</div>
				</li>
	
				<li class="faq_item" role="listitem">
					<h3 class="faq_item_q">
						<button type="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq_item1" data-omni-type="microsite_contentinter" data-omni="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:faq^6:expand:6" ga-ca="content click" ga-ac="feature" ga-la="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:faq^6:expand:6">Какой дисплей у Galaxy&nbsp;S22?</button>
					</h3>
					<div class="faq_item_a" id="faq_item1">
						
						<p>Galaxy&nbsp;S22 Ultra может похвастаться 6,8-дюймовым дисплеем Edge Quad HD+ Dynamic AMOLED 2X с технологией Vision Booster. Это наш самый впечатляющий дисплей с увеличенной на 16% яркостью и коэффициентом контрастности 3 000 000:1. А частота обновления 120 Гц обеспечивает суперплавный скроллинг, подстраиваясь под изображение на экране для оптимального просмотра.</p>
						
						
						<a href="#display" class="c_btn_f3 btn_big btn_bg_empty" title="" data-omni-type="microsite_contentinter" data-omni="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:faq^6:jump:vision-booster" ga-ca="content click" ga-ac="feature" ga-la="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:faq^6:jump:vision-booster">
							<span class="c_btn_area"><span class="copy">ПЕРЕЙТИ К ДИСПЛЕЮ</span></span>
						</a>
					</div>
				</li>
	
				<li class="faq_item" role="listitem">
					<h3 class="faq_item_q">

					</h3>
					<div class="faq_item_a" id="faq_item1">
						<p>Galaxy&nbsp;S22 Ultra — отличный телефон для тех, кто хочет насладиться мобильными играми премиум-класса, поскольку он оснащен быстрым 4-нм процессором, аккумулятором с длительным сроком службы и большим объемом памяти.</p>
						<a href="#performance" class="c_btn_f3 btn_big btn_bg_empty" title="" data-omni-type="microsite_contentinter" data-omni="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:faq^7:jump:performance" ga-ca="content click" ga-ac="feature" ga-la="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:faq^7:jump:performance">

					<h3 class="faq_item_q">
						<button type="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq_item1" data-omni-type="microsite_contentinter" data-omni="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:faq^8:expand:8" ga-ca="content click" ga-ac="feature" ga-la="galaxy-s22-ultra:highlights:faq^8:expand:8">Подходит ли Galaxy&nbsp;S22 Ultra для профессиональных фотографий?</button>
					</h3>
					<div class="faq_item_a" id="faq_item1">
						<p>Профессиональная камера Galaxy&nbsp;S22 Ultra дополнена рядом революционных улучшений: функция Ночной режим для съемки в темное время суток, большой пиксельный сенсор, сверхпрозрачное стекло и линзы, функции Detail Enhancer, Auto Framerate, Super Night Solution и Adaptive Pixel.</p>

<script>
window.GALAXY_IS_ASYNC=true;
;(function(win,doc,callback){'use strict';callback=callback||function(){};function detach(){if(doc.addEventListener){doc.removeEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',completed)}else{doc.detachEvent('onreadystatechange',completed)}}function completed(){if(doc.addEventListener||event.type==='load'||doc.readyState==='complete'){detach();callback(window,window.jQuery)}}function init(){if (doc.addEventListener){doc.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',completed)}else{doc.attachEvent('onreadystatechange',completed)}}init()})(window,document,function(win,$){
$.ajaxSetup({cache:true});
$.ajax('/samsung/resources/global/galaxy-s22-ultra/common/js/plugins.min.js')
.then(function(){return $.ajax('/samsung/resources/global/galaxy-s22-ultra/common/js/common.min.js')})
.then(function(){return $.ajax('/samsung/resources/global/galaxy-s22-ultra/common/js/localization/common.min.js')})
.then(function(){return $.ajax('/samsung/resources/global/galaxy-s22-ultra/common/js/3d/polyfills.min.js')})
.then(function(){


	//
//<!-- 3. Javascript -->

const disclaimer = function() {
	if ( !$('#desc-section').length ) { return false; }

	const $disclaimer = $('#desc-section');
	const anthorTitle = $disclaimer.find('ol').data('title') || '';

	const addEvent = function() {
		$(document).off('click.disclaimer').on('click.disclaimer', 'a.click_sup', action);
	};

	const action = function(e) {
		let subnavHeight = $('#subnav, .floating-navigation__inner').height();
		let $target = $( this.getAttribute('href') );
		let moveTop = $target.offset().top - subnavHeight - 40; // padding-top 40;
		let $accessibility;

		$target.wrapInner( $('<a />', {attr: {'tabindex': 0}}) );
		$accessibility = $target.find('a');
		$accessibility.focus().one('blur', function() { $target.html( $accessibility.html() ); });

		GALAXY.setScrollTop( moveTop );

		e.preventDefault();
	};

	const addAnthor = function() {
		let $sup = $(this);
		let val = $sup.html().split(',');
		let lens = val.length;
		let i=0, arr=[];
		for (;i<lens;i++) {
			let num = val[i].replace(/\s/g,'');
			arr.push('<a href="#disclaimer'+num+'" class="click_sup" title="'+anthorTitle+'">'+ num +'</a>');
		}
		$sup.html(arr.join(','));
	};

	const init = function() {
		let $sup = $('article[class^=m_feature] sup:not(.default)');
		$disclaimer.find('li').each(function(i) {
			this.id = 'disclaimer' + (this.dataset.sup || i+1);
		});
		$sup.each(addAnthor);
	};

	init();
	addEvent();
};

const focusInView = function() {
	let scrollValueCheck = null;
	const onAction = function(e) {
		if ( e.keyCode == 9 ) {
			let target = this.dataset.focusVsTarget || this;
			let $target = $(target);
			let scrollValue = $target.offset().top - GALAXY.areaHeight/2;
			GALAXY.setScrollTop( scrollValue );
			clearTimeout(scrollValueCheck);
			scrollValueCheck = setTimeout(function(){
				if ( GALAXY.scrollTop != scrollValueCheck ) {
					GALAXY.setScrollTop( scrollValue );
				}
			},50);
			if (!$target.parents('article').hasClass('not-focus-able')) {
				document.documentElement.classList.add('focus-able');
			}else {
				document.documentElement.classList.remove('focus-able');
			}
		}
	};

	$('#contents, .m_dotcom_footer').find('a, button, input, select').on('keyup.focusInView', onAction);
	$('#subnav').find('a, button, input, select').off('keyup.focusInView', onAction);

	$('#contents').on('click.focusInView', function () {
		document.documentElement.classList.remove('focus-able');
	});
	$('#contents').on('keyup.enterInView', function (e) {
		if (e.keyCode == 13 ) document.documentElement.classList.add('focus-able');
	});
};

const bannerColumn = function() {
	$('.m_feature_banners').each(function() {
		let visibleLens = $(this).find('>:visible').length;
		$(this).removeClass('column1 column2 column3').addClass('column' + visibleLens);
	});

	$('.m_feature_jump').each(function() {
		let $jump = $(this);
		let $list = $('.jump_contents>ul');
		let $card = $list.find('.jump_card:visible');
		let $cardAnchor = $list.find('.jump_card a');
		let $prev = $('.jump_arrows a.prev');
		let $next = $('.jump_arrows a.next');
		let lens = $card.length;
		let maxView = 5;

		const obImageLazy = function(entries, observer) {
			$.each(entries, function(i, entry) {
				if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
					let $images = $(entry.target).find('img');
					$images.data('lazy', false);
					bannerResize(true);
					observer.unobserve( entry.target );
				}
			});
		}
		const bannerResize = function(force) {
			if ( force || (GALAXY.sizeMode && GALAXY.sizeMode != GALAXY.prevSizeMode)) {
				$card.each(function(i, li) {
					let $image = $(li).find('img');
					if ($image.data('lazy') == false) {
						let imageUrl = GALAXY.setMediaBaseURL(GALAXY.getImageSources($image)[GALAXY.sizeMode]);
						if (typeof imageUrl == 'string') {
							$image.attr({'src': imageUrl });
						}
					}
				});
			}
		}
		const obImageInstance = new IntersectionObserver(obImageLazy, {root: null, rootMargin: '300%', thresholder: [0]});
		obImageInstance.observe( this );

		const slide = {
			init: false,
			index: 0,
			animation: false,
			interavl: null,
			maxView: (lens - maxView),
			prev: function(e) {
				if ( slide.animation ) { return false; }
				slide.animation = true;
				if ( slide.index == 0 ) {
					slide.animation = false;
					return false;
				}
				slide.index = slide.index - 1;
				slide.action();
				if(e) e.preventDefault();
			},
			next: function(e) {
				if ( slide.animation ) { return false; }
				slide.animation = true;
				if ( slide.index >= slide.maxView ) {
					slide.animation = false;
					return false;
				}
				slide.index = slide.index + 1;
				slide.action();
				if(e) e.preventDefault();
			},
			checkFocus : function (direction) {
				if (direction === 'next') slide.next();
				if (direction === 'prev') slide.prev();
			},
			action: function() {
				slide.animation = true;
				slide.btnVisibleCheck();

				let w = $card.width() + parseInt($card.eq(1).css('margin-left'));
				$list.__css({x: -w * slide.index});
				GALAXY.setTransitionEndEvent($list, slide.end)
			},
			btnVisibleCheck: function() {
				$prev.decideClass('hide', (slide.index == 0));
				$next.decideClass('hide', (slide.index >= slide.maxView));
			},
			end: function() {
				slide.animation = false;
			}
		}

		if ( lens > 4 ) {
			$jump.addClass('cols5');
			if ( lens > 4){
				slide.init = true;
				$('.m_feature_jump .jump_arrows').show();
				slide.index = Math.max(($card.filter('.on').index()+1 - maxView), 0);
				slide.action();
				slide.btnVisibleCheck();
				$prev.on('click', slide.prev);
				$next.on('click', slide.next);
				$cardAnchor.on('keydown', function (e) {
					if (e.keyCode === 9) {
						if (e.shiftKey) {
							slide.checkFocus('prev');
						}else {
							slide.checkFocus('next');
						}
					}
				});
			}
		} else {
			$jump.addClass('cols4');
			$card.each(function(i, li) {
				let $image = $(li).find('img').data('lazy', true);
				if (i==0) {
					$image.attr({ 'data-media-s1': $image.attr('data-media-s1').replace('_s.png','_s.png') })
				}
				$image.attr({ 'data-media-s4': $image.attr('data-media-s4').replace('.png', '-v2.png') })
			});
		}

		GALAXY.resize(function() {
			if ( slide.init && GALAXY.sizeMode > 2) {
				slide.interavl && clearTimeout(slide.interavl);
				slide.interavl = setTimeout(slide.action, 150);
			}
			bannerResize();
		});
		bannerResize(true);
	});
};

// floating navigator bug
const floaingNaviScroll = function() {
	const onScroll = function() {
		// let scrollTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
		let oFloatNaviElement = document.querySelector('.floating-navigation');
		let offsetTop = oFloatNaviElement.getBoundingClientRect().top;
		let className = 'new-floating-navigation--fixed';
		oFloatNaviElement.classList[(offsetTop < 0)?'add':'remove'](className);
	};
	window.addEventListener('scroll', onScroll, { passive: true });
};
$('.floating-navigation').length && floaingNaviScroll();

	if (typeof _satellite != 'undefined' && value) {
		_satellite.setVar('scrollTrack', value);
		_satellite.track('section_scroll_end');
	}
};

const getDotcomNavH = function () {
	if (!GALAXY.isGalaxy) {
		let gnbH = $('.gnb').height() || 0;
		let floatingNavH = $('.floating-navigation__wrap').height() || 0;
		return (gnbH+floatingNavH);
	}else {
		return 0;
	}
}

const faveScroll = function faveScroll(callback, ease) {
	var easing = 1 - (ease || 0);
	var $window = $(window);
	var scrollTop = 0;
	var lastScrollTop = 0;
	var checkScrolled = false;
	var interavl = null;

	if (!callback) {
		throw Error('Invalid required arguments Callback Function');
	}

	window.cancelAnimationFrame(onUpdate);

	function onUpdate() {
		var scrollY = window.pageYOffset;
		scrollTop += (scrollY - scrollTop) * easing;

		if (Math.abs(scrollY - scrollTop) < easing) {
		scrollTop = scrollY;
		} else {
		interavl = window.requestAnimationFrame(onUpdate);
		}

		callback.call(this, scrollTop);
	}

	return function () {
		interavl = window.requestAnimationFrame(onUpdate);
	};
};

const faqList = function() {
	let $section = $('.m_faq-banner'),
		$item_q, $item_a, $item_btns;
	const omni = { open: ':expand:', close: ':collapse:' };

	const asset = function() {
		$item_q = $section.find('.faq_item_q');
		$item_a = $section.find('.faq_item_a');
		$item_btns = $item_q.find('button');
	}

	const bindEvent = function() {
		$item_btns.off('click').on('click', showContent);
	}

	const init = function() {
		if ( !$section.length ) { return false; }

		asset();
		bindEvent();
		let setTime1;
		let setTime2;
		$section[0].querySelectorAll('.c_btn_f3').forEach(function (_this) {
			_this.addEventListener('click', function () {
				let thisAnchor = this.href.split('#')[1];
				let targetAnchor = document.querySelector('#'+thisAnchor);
				clearTimeout(setTime1);
				clearTimeout(setTime2);
				
				if(targetAnchor.tagName == 'H2' || targetAnchor.tagName == 'H3') {
					targetAnchor.setAttribute('tabindex', 0);
					setTime1 = setTimeout(function(){
						targetAnchor.focus();
					},600);
				}else {
					$(targetAnchor).find('h2,h3').attr('tabindex',0);
					setTime1 = setTimeout(function(){
						$(targetAnchor).find('h2,h3').focus();
					},600);
				}
			});
		})

		return this;
	}

	const showContent = function() {
		const $item_btn = $(this);
		const curIndex = $item_btns.index(this);
		const $item = $item_btn.closest('.faq_item');
		const omniture = this.dataset.omni;

		if ( !$item.hasClass('is-open') ) {
			$item.addClass('is-open');
			$item_btn.attr({
				'aria-expanded': 'true',
				'ga-la': omniture.replace(omni.open, omni.close),
				'data-omni': omniture.replace(omni.open, omni.close)
			});
			$item_a.eq(curIndex).stop().slideDown(300);
		} else {
			$item.removeClass('is-open');
			$item_btn.attr({
				'aria-expanded': 'false',
				'ga-la': omniture.replace(omni.close, omni.open),
				'data-omni': omniture.replace(omni.close, omni.open)
			});
			$item_a.eq(curIndex).stop().slideUp(300);
		}
		GALAXY.omniture(omniture);
		return false;
	}
	init();
};

const copyChangePosition = (function () {
	let articles;
	let imgLoaded = false;
	let setIntervalImgLoad;

    const init = function() {
		articles = document.querySelectorAll('article[class*="m_feature-"]');
        this.resize();
    }

    const changeTablet = function(mobile) {
        articles.forEach(function(_this) {
			let cloneData = _this.querySelector('.o_clone-content');
			let targetData = _this.querySelector('.o_clone-target');

			if (cloneData && targetData) {
				let cloneNodes = (mobile) ? cloneData.cloneNode(true) : targetData.cloneNode(true);
				let cloneNodesLen = (mobile) ? cloneData.children.length : targetData.children.length;
				let apeendArea = (mobile) ? targetData : cloneData;
				let removeArea = (mobile) ? cloneData : targetData;
				
				for(let i=0;i < cloneNodesLen; i++) {apeendArea.appendChild(cloneNodes.children[0]);}
				
				let $images = apeendArea.querySelectorAll('img');

				setIntervalImgLoad = setInterval(function () {
					if (window.pageYOffset > 10 && !imgLoaded) {
						imgLoad($images);
					}else {
						clearInterval(setIntervalImgLoad);
					}
				},1000);

				removeArea.innerHTML = '';
			}
		});
    }
	const imgLoad = function (img) {
		setTimeout(function () {
			imgLoaded = true;
		},500);
		img.forEach(function (_this) {
			_this.setAttribute('src', GALAXY.getImageSources($(_this))[GALAXY.sizeMode]);
		});
	}

	const resize = function () {
		if ( !GALAXY.sizeMode || !articles.length ) return false;

        if ( (GALAXY.sizeMode < 2) ) {
			changeTablet(true);
        } else if ( GALAXY.sizeMode > 1 ) {
			changeTablet(false);
        }
	}

	return {
		init : init,
		resize : resize
	}
})();

const sectionScrollMask = (function () {
	let section;
	let startNum = 100;
	let startAction = (window.innerHeight/4);
	const init = function () {
		section = document.querySelectorAll('.section-fixed-wrap');
		section.forEach(function (_this,index) {
			let blankDiv = document.createElement('div');
			blankDiv.setAttribute('class', 'fixed-blank');
			_this.parentNode.insertBefore(blankDiv,_this);
		});
		this.scroll();
	}
	const scroll = function () {
		if (section) {
			section.forEach(function (_this,index) {
				let fixedBlank = _this.previousSibling;
				let currentScroll = window.pageYOffset - (fixedBlank.offsetTop+_this.clientHeight-window.innerHeight);

				let _offset = (window.pageYOffset - (fixedBlank.offsetTop+_this.clientHeight-window.innerHeight));
				let _height = (_this.clientHeight - window.innerHeight);
				let percent = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, _offset / _height));

				if(currentScroll >= -(startNum-getDotcomNavH()) + startAction && currentScroll<= window.innerHeight+getDotcomNavH()){
					fixed(_this,fixedBlank,percent);
				}else {
					if(!document.documentElement.classList.contains('no-scroll')) nonFixed(_this,fixedBlank);
				}
			});
		}
	}
	const fixed = function (_this,fixedBlank,percent) {
		fixedBlank.style.paddingTop = _this.clientHeight + 'px';

		_this.style.position = 'fixed';
		_this.style.left = '50%';
		_this.style.transform = 'translateX(-50%)';

		_this.style.bottom = ((-startNum + (startNum * percent))+startAction) + 'px'

		if(_this.querySelector('[data-end-sticky="true"]')) _this.querySelector('[data-end-sticky="true"]').classList.add('end-sticky');
	}
	const nonFixed = function (_this,fixedBlank) {
		fixedBlank.style.paddingTop = 0 + 'px';

		_this.style.position = 'relative';
		_this.style.left = 0;
		_this.style.transform = '';

		_this.style.bottom = 0;

		if(_this.querySelector('[data-end-sticky="true"]')) _this.querySelector('[data-end-sticky="true"]').classList.remove('end-sticky');
	}
	const resize = function () {
		startNum = ( GALAXY.sizeMode > 1 ) ? 100 : 25;
		startAction = (window.innerHeight/4);
		this.scroll();
	}

	return {
		init : init,
		scroll : scroll,
		resize : resize
	}
})();

const videoScroll = function (el) {
	let _video;
	let prograss = 0;
	let loadSetInterval;
	let loaded = false;
	let videoImwidthArr = ['', '?imwidth=1280', ''];
	let videoImwidth;
	const init = function () {
		load();

		loadSetInterval = setInterval(function () {
			if (_video.buffered.length) {
				let percent = (_video.buffered.end(0) / _video.duration);

				loaded = true;
				clearInterval(loadSetInterval);
				if(document.querySelector('.design-video-wrap')) document.querySelector('.design-video-wrap').classList.add('show');
				if(document.querySelector('.m_feature-spen')) document.querySelector('.m_feature-spen').classList.add('show');
			}
		},100);
	}
	const load = function () {
		let videoSrc = el.querySelector('video').getAttribute('data-src').split('.mp4')[0];

		if (GALAXY.sizeMode == 3 || GALAXY.sizeMode == 4) videoImwidth = videoImwidthArr[0];
		if (GALAXY.sizeMode == 2) videoImwidth = videoImwidthArr[1];
		if (GALAXY.sizeMode == 1) {
			videoImwidth = videoImwidthArr[2];
			videoSrc = videoSrc + '_s';
		}

		videoSrc = (document.documentElement.classList.contains('sH')) ? videoSrc + '.mp4?imbypass=true'+ videoImwidth : videoSrc + '_low.mp4?imbypass=true' + videoImwidth;
		el.querySelector('video source').setAttribute('src',videoSrc);
		_video = el.querySelector('video');
		_video.load();
	}
	const draw = function (percent) {
		if (loaded) {
			if (percent != undefined) prograss = percent;
			if(_video.duration) {
				_video.currentTime = (prograss*(_video.duration-0.1));
			}
		}
	}
	const scroll = function (percent) {
		draw(percent);
	}
	const resize = function () {
		if ( GALAXY.sizeMode && GALAXY.sizeMode != GALAXY.prevSizeMode ) {
			load();
		}
		draw(prograss);
	}

	return {
		init : init,
		draw : draw,
		scroll : scroll,
		resize : resize
	}
}

const outHeightNode = function () {
	document.querySelectorAll('.outH').forEach(function (_this) {
		if ( document.documentElement.classList.contains('mobile')) _this.style.height = (window.outerHeight+getDotcomNavH()) + 'px';
	});
}

function videoReplayTitle() {
	$('#contents .m_video-wrap').each(function(){
		const $video = $(this).find('video');
		const $btnPlay = $(this).find('.btn_vod_ctrl');
		$video.off('ended.article').on('ended.article', function () {
			$btnPlay.addClass('btn-startover');
			$btnPlay.find('span').text($btnPlay.data('replay-title'));
		});
	});
}

	}
});

});


function toggleSticky(section, options) {
	const minH = parseInt(section.__css('min-height')) || 800;
	if (GALAXY.areaHeight > minH) {
		section.hasClass('motion-off') && section.removeClass('motion-off');
		section.find('.sticky-wrap').data('faveSticky') && section.find('.sticky-wrap').data('faveSticky').destroy();
		section.find('.sticky-wrap').faveSticky(options);
	} else {
		!section.hasClass('motion-off') && section.addClass('motion-off');
		section.find('.sticky-wrap').data('faveSticky') && section.find('.sticky-wrap').data('faveSticky').destroy();
	}
}

const arModal = (function() {
	const init = function() {
		if ( !$('.__ar__button').hasClass('__on') ) {
			$('.__ar__button > a.__link').each(function() {
				let $button = $(this).find('.c_btn_f3');
				let buttonClass = $button.data('class');
				$button.replaceWith($('<button type="button" class="'+buttonClass+'">'+ $button.html() +'</button>'));
				$(this).replaceWith($('<article class="__link">'+ this.innerHTML +'</article>'));
			});
		}
	}

	return {
		init: init
	}
})().init();



function getCurPercent(scr, startPoint, Movearea, totalArea){
	var _per = (scr - (totalArea*startPoint)) / (totalArea*Movearea);
	_per = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, _per))
	return _per;
}

GALAXY.isSticky = $.support.sticky;
$('html').decideClass('sticky', GALAXY.isSticky);

var isEdge = (/Edge\//i).test(navigator.userAgent);
var isNewEdge = (/Edg\//i).test(navigator.userAgent);

var faveSticky = function(el, option){
	var $el = $(el);
	var $window = $(window);
	var $html = $('html');
	var windowH = $window.height();
	var $stickyInner = $el.find('.sticky-inner');
    var elTop = $el.offset().top;
	var elH = $el.height();
	var innerH = $stickyInner.height();
	var _moveArea;
	var _positionTop;
	var onceFlag = false;
	var defaults = {
		supportIE: true,
		top: 'auto',
		preShow: 0,
		postShow : 0,
		marginTop : null,
		on: function(){},
		onScroll: function(){},
		off: function(){},
		onResize: function(){},
		fadeIn: null,
		easeScroll : false,
		easeDuration : 0
	}
	var options = $.extend({}, defaults, option);
	var nowHeight = $(window).height();
	var prevScrDir = 0;
	var scrDir = 0;
	var _flag = false;
	var isKill = false;
	var resizeScr, resizePer, initData;
	var staticMode = false;
	var optionPreShow;
	var optionPostShow;
	var globalScrollY;

  var _init = function () {
		preShowFunc();
		offClass();

		if ( !options.supportIE && ( $html.hasClass('ie') || isEdge ) )  { return false; }
		setVar();
		checkNav();
		setPosition();
		scroll();
		GALAXY.resize(resize, true);
		if(options.easeScroll) {
			window.addEventListener('scroll', faveScroll(scroll, options.easeDuration));
		}else {
			GALAXY.scroll(function () {
				if(!staticMode) scroll(GALAXY.scrollTop);
			});
		}
	};

	var checkNav = function(){
		var navH = $('#subnav, .floating-navigation__wrap').height() || 0;
		return navH;
	};
	
	var preShowFunc = function () {
		optionPreShow = ($html.hasClass('ie')) ? 0 : (window.innerHeight * options.preShow);
	}
	var getPostShow = function () {
		optionPostShow = ($html.hasClass('ie')) ? 0 : (window.innerHeight * options.postShow);
		return optionPostShow;
	}

	var setPosition = function (){
		var contH = $stickyInner.outerHeight();
		var align = options.top;
		var posTop = parseInt($stickyInner.css('top'));
		var subNavH = checkNav();

		switch ( align ) {
			case 'auto':
				posTop = null;
				break;

			case 'top':
				posTop = subNavH;
				break;

			case 'center':
				posTop = ((windowH + subNavH) - contH) / 2;
				break;

			case 'bottom':
				posTop = (windowH - contH);
				break;

			default:
				posTop = parseInt(align);
				break;
		}
		$stickyInner.css('top', posTop);
		_positionTop = posTop;
	};

	var _positionTopFn = function(){
		return _positionTop;
	}

	var scrollPosition = function(){
		var _initPos, _startPos, _endPos, _baseShow, _ieEndPos, _fadeInPos,
			scrollTop = (GALAXY.prevSizeMode) ? globalScrollY : $window.scrollTop();
			elTop = (elTop != $el.offset().top) ? elTop = $el.offset().top : elTop;
			_moveArea = elH - innerH + getPostShow();

		if (optionPreShow){
			_baseShow = parseInt(optionPreShow);
		}else{
			_baseShow = (_positionTop < 0 ) ? 0 : _positionTop;
		}

		_initPos = scrollTop >= elTop - (windowH + (windowH/2)) && scrollTop <= elTop + elH;
		_startPos = ($html.hasClass('ie')) ? scrollTop >= (elTop - _baseShow) : scrollTop >= elTop - (windowH + (windowH/2)) && scrollTop <= elTop + elH;
		_endPos = scrollTop > elTop + elH + optionPreShow;
		_ieEndPos = scrollTop > elTop + elH - innerH - _positionTop;
		_fadeInPos = scrollTop >= (elTop - windowH) && scrollTop <= elTop - _positionTop;
		
		return {
			init: _initPos,
			on: _startPos,
			off: _endPos,
			ieEnd: _ieEndPos,
			baseShow: _baseShow,
			fadeInPos: _fadeInPos
		}
	}

	var scrollInit = function () {
		if( GALAXY.isSticky && !isEdge ) {
			$html.addClass('is-sticky');
		}else{
			$html.addClass('is-fixed');
		}
		_moveArea = elH - innerH + getPostShow();
		options.on.call($el);
		setLowPosition();
		$el.data('sticky-init', true);
		initData = $el.data('sticky-init');

		if(options.fadeIn){
			$stickyInner.css('opacity', 0);
		}
		function setLowPosition(){
			if($stickyInner.outerHeight() != innerH){
				setVar();
				setPosition();
				window.caf(setLowPosition);
			}else{
				!initData && window.raf(setLowPosition);
			}
		}
	};

    var scroll = function (scrollY) {
		globalScrollY = scrollY;
		var scrPosition = scrollPosition();
		var isInit = scrPosition.init;
		var isShow = scrPosition.on;
		var isHide = scrPosition.off;
		var isIeEnd = scrPosition.ieEnd;
		var _percent = 0;
		var _scrollTop = 0;
		var isData = $el.data('faveSticky');
		var initData = $el.data('sticky-init');

		if ( isInit ) {
			if( !initData ){ scrollInit(); }
			if( isShow ){
				_scrollTop = scrollY - elTop + scrPosition.baseShow;
				if(optionPreShow){
					_percent = Math.min(1, _scrollTop / (_moveArea + scrPosition.baseShow - _positionTop));
				}else{
					_positionTop = (_positionTop < 0) ? 0 : _positionTop;
					_percent = Math.min(1, _scrollTop / (_moveArea - _positionTop));
				}
				if( GALAXY.isSticky && !isEdge ) {$html.addClass('is-sticky');}

				$el.addClass('sticky-in');
				_percent = Math.min(1, Math.max(0, _percent)).toFixed(3);
				onceFlag = false;

				if( $html.hasClass('ie') || isEdge ){
					if(isIeEnd){
						$el.addClass('sticky-end');
					}else{
						$el.removeClass('sticky-end');
					}
				}

				isData && options.onScroll.call($el, _percent, _scrollTop);

			}else{
				if( $html.hasClass('ie') || isEdge ) { $el.removeClass('sticky-in'); }

				if(!scrDir && !_flag){
					_flag = true;
					_percent = '0';
					isData && options.onScroll.call($el, _percent, _scrollTop);
				}
				if(scrDir){
					_flag = false;
				}
			}

			if(options.fadeIn && scrPosition.fadeInPos){
				var _scrollTop = scrollY - elTop + windowH;
				var _percent = Math.min(1, _scrollTop / (windowH - _positionTop));
				$stickyInner.css('opacity', _percent);
			}

			getScrDirection();

		}else {
			$el.removeClass('sticky-in');
			$el.data('sticky-init', false);
		}

		if(isHide && !onceFlag){
			onceFlag = true;
			options.off.call($el);
		}

		resizeScr = _scrollTop;
		resizePer = _percent;
	}

	function getScrDirection(){
		scrDir = prevScrDir <= globalScrollY;

		if( prevScrDir != globalScrollY){
			prevScrDir = globalScrollY;
		}
	}

	var _moveAreaFn = function(){
		return _moveArea;
	}

	var setVar = function(){
		elTop = $el.offset().top;
		elH = $el.height();
		innerH = $stickyInner.outerHeight();
		windowH = $window.height();
		$el.data('sticky-init', false);
	}

	var resize = function () {
		if(isKill) return false;
		preShowFunc();

		options.onResize.call($el);
		if( GALAXY.prevSizeMode && GALAXY.prevSizeMode != GALAXY.sizeMode ){
			setVar();
			setPosition();
			checkNav();
			scroll();
			options.onScroll.call($el, resizeScr, resizePer);
		}
		
		var prevHeight = nowHeight;
		nowHeight = $(window).height();
		if(nowHeight != prevHeight){
			setVar();
			setPosition();
			scroll();
			options.onResize.call($el);
			options.onScroll.call($el, resizeScr, resizePer);
		}

		offClass();
	}
	var  getMinHeight = function () {
		let s4MH = $stickyInner.attr('data-minHeight-s4') || 10,
			s3MH = $stickyInner.attr('data-minHeight-s3') || s4MH,
			s2MH = $stickyInner.attr('data-minHeight-s2') || s3MH,
			s1MH = $stickyInner.attr('data-minHeight-s1') || s2MH;

		return [null, s1MH, s2MH, s3MH, s4MH]
	}
	var offClass = function () {
		staticMode = (nowHeight > getMinHeight()[GALAXY.sizeMode]) ? false : true;
		var $parent = $el.parent();
		if (staticMode) {
			!$parent.hasClass('motion-off') && $parent.addClass('motion-off');
		} else {
			$parent.hasClass('motion-off') && $parent.removeClass('motion-off');
		}
	}

	var reset = function(){
		$stickyInner.removeAttr('style');
		$el.removeClass('sticky-in');
	};

	var _destroy = function(){
		reset();
		$el.data('faveSticky', undefined);
		isKill = true;
	};

	var _reInit = function (opt) {
		var reOptions = opt || options;
		$el.data('faveSticky') && _init();
		options = $.extend({}, defaults, reOptions);
	}

	_init();

    return {
		el: $el,
		moveArea: _moveAreaFn,
		top: _positionTopFn,
		destroy: _destroy,
		scroll: scroll,
		init: _init,
		resize: resize,
		reInit: _reInit,
		wrapH: elH,
		wrapTop: elTop,
		scr: globalScrollY,
		innerH: innerH

    }

}

$.fn.faveSticky = function(options){
	return this.each(function () {
		var $this = $(this);
		if ( $this.data('faveSticky') != null ) {
			$this.data('faveSticky').reInit();
		} else {
			$this.data('faveSticky', new faveSticky(this, options));
		}
	});
}



const SEQUENCE = function (el,option) {
	const canvas = el;
	let ctx;

	let sequenceArray;
	let canvasW = 0;
	let canvasH = 0;
	let prograss = 0;

	let widthRatio;
	let heightRatio;

	let _left = 0;
	let _top = 0;
	let _width = 0;
	let _height = 0;
	let requestFrame;
	let playing = false;
	let loaded = false;
	let playFrame = 0;
	let rowBand = false;

	let _src = option.src || '';
	let _frame = option.frame || 0;
	let _speed = option.speed || 0.01;
	let _zeroLength = option.zeroLength || 3;
	let _type = option.type || 'jpg';
	let _parent = option.parent || '';
	let _maxFrame = option.maxFrame || _frame;

	let totalFrame;
	let startEventTrue = false;
	let endEventTrue = false;

	const countZero = function (i) {
		let cnt;
		let zeroText = '';
		for (var j = 0; j < (_zeroLength - i.toString().length); j++) zeroText += '0';
		cnt = zeroText+i;
		return cnt;
	}
	let seqLoadInterval;
	const load = function () {
		if (!loaded) {
			rowBand = document.documentElement.classList.contains('sL');
			let increaseNum = (!rowBand) ? 1 : 2;
			totalFrame = (_maxFrame/increaseNum);

			sequenceArray = [];
			ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
			let loadImgCount = 0;

			let i = 0;
			seqLoadInterval = setInterval(function () {
				i += increaseNum;
				let sequenceImg = new Image();
				sequenceImg.src = _src + countZero(i) + '.' + _type;

				sequenceImg.onload = function () {
					loadImgCount++;
					// 1st load
					if (loadImgCount === 1) firstImgLoad(sequenceImg);
					// complete load
					if (loadImgCount === totalFrame) allImgLoad();
				}
				sequenceArray.push({
					idx : i, 
					img : sequenceImg
				});
				if (i >= _frame) clearInterval(seqLoadInterval);
			},2);
		}
	}

	const firstImgLoad = function (img) {
		widthRatio = (img.naturalWidth / img.naturalHeight);
		heightRatio = (img.naturalHeight / img.naturalWidth);
		resize();
		imgDraw(sequenceArray[0].img);
	}

	const allImgLoad = function () {
		loaded = true;
		draw(prograss);
	}

	const draw = function (percent) {
		prograss = percent;
		playFrame = prograss;
		let index = Math.floor(totalFrame*prograss);

		// start
		if (prograss > 0 && loaded && !startEventTrue) {
			startEventTrue = true;
			option.startEvent && option.startEvent.call();
		}
		// startReset
		if (prograss === 0 && loaded && startEventTrue) {
			startEventTrue = false;
			option.startResetEvent && option.startResetEvent.call();
		}
		
		// end
		if (prograss === 1 && loaded && !endEventTrue) {
			endEventTrue = true;
			option.endEvent && option.endEvent.call();
		}
		// endReset
		if (prograss < 1 && loaded && endEventTrue) {
			endEventTrue = false;
			option.endResetEvent && option.endResetEvent.call();
		}

		if (loaded && sequenceArray[index]) imgDraw(sequenceArray[index].img);
	}

	const imgDraw = function (el) {
		canvas.width = canvas.width;
		ctx.beginPath();
		ctx.drawImage(el,_left,_top,_width,_height);
		ctx.closePath();
	}

	const play = function () {
		const playRequest = function () {
			if (playFrame < 1) {
				draw(playFrame);
				playFrame += _speed;
				requestFrame = window.requestAnimationFrame(playRequest);
			} else {
				stop({reset : false});
			}
		}

		if (!playing) {
			playing = true;
			playRequest();
		}
	}

	const pause = function () {
		playing = false;
		window.cancelAnimationFrame(requestFrame);
	}
	
	const stop = function (reset) {
		playFrame = 0;
		pause();

		if (reset.reset) {
			draw(0);
		} else {
			option.endEvent && option.endEvent.call();
		}
	}

	const scroll = function (p) {
		draw(p);
	}

	const resize = function () {
		canvasW = _parent.clientWidth || window.innerWidth;
		canvasH = _parent.clientHeight || window.innerHeight;
		canvas.width = canvasW;
		canvas.height = canvasH;

		_left = (canvasW < canvasH) ? 0 : (canvasW/2) - (canvasH * widthRatio/2) ;
		_top = (canvasW < canvasH) ? (canvasH/2) - (canvasW * heightRatio/2) : 0;
		_width = (canvasW < canvasH) ? canvasW : (canvasH * widthRatio);
		_height = (canvasW < canvasH) ? (canvasW * heightRatio) : canvasH;

		draw(prograss);
	}

	const destroy = function () {
		if (loaded) {
			loaded = false;
			canvas.width = canvas.width;
			window.cancelAnimationFrame(requestFrame);
			ctx = '';
		}
	}

	return {
		load : load,
		draw : draw,
		play : play,
		pause : pause,
		stop : stop,
		scroll : scroll,
		resize : resize,
		destroy : destroy
	}
}

const excellenceMotion = (function () {
	const excellence = document.querySelector('.m_content-excellence');
	const excellenceList = document.querySelector('.excellence-list');
	const excellenceListUl = excellenceList.querySelector('ul');
	const excellenceMobileMove = excellenceList.querySelector('.mobile-move');
	const excellenceTitle = excellence.querySelector('.f_header-type1');
	let eCard = excellenceList.querySelectorAll('.e-card');

	let _this;
	let totalW = 0;
	let excellenceSticky;
	let cloneList;
	let arrowClick = false;
	let blankDiv;

	const init = function () {
		_this = this;
		_this.resize();

		stickyMotion();
		slideMotion();
	}

	// excellence sticky
	const stickyMotion = function () {
		let titleL = 0;
		let totalH = 0;
		let titleW = 0;
		let progress = 0;

		const _init = function () {
			cloneList = excellenceListUl.cloneNode(true);
			cloneList.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
			cloneList.classList.add('clone-list');
			excellenceList.appendChild(cloneList);

			blankDiv = document.createElement('div');
			blankDiv.classList.add('blank-div');
			excellenceList.appendChild(blankDiv);

			_resize();

			excellence.style.marginTop = (totalH/2) + 'px';
			if (!document.documentElement.classList.contains('ie11')) {
				excellence.querySelector('.sticky-inner').style.transform = 'translateY('+(-totalH/2)+'px)';
			}else {
				excellence.querySelector('.sticky-inner').style.marginTop = (-totalH/2) + 'px';
			}
		}
		let moveArea;
		const _option = {
			top: 'center',
			onScroll: function(percent, scroll){
				_scroll(scroll);
			},
			onResize: function(){
				moveArea = excellenceSticky.data('faveSticky').moveArea();
				_this.resize();
				_resize();
				_scroll(progress);
			}
		}

		const _scroll = function (scroll) {
			let p = getCurPercent(scroll, 0, 1, moveArea);

			let distance;
			if(!document.documentElement.classList.contains('rtl')) {
				distance = titleL - ((totalW-titleW)*p);
			}else {
				distance = -titleL + ((totalW-titleW)*p);
			}
			if(!document.documentElement.classList.contains('s1')) _this.move(distance);
		}

		const _jump = function (idx) {
			let percent = (idx/eCard.length);
			let fakeDiv = (excellence.clientHeight-window.innerHeight)*percent;
			setTimeout(function () {
				window.scrollTo(0,(excellence.offsetTop + fakeDiv));
			},300);
		}

		const _keyup = function (el, idx) {
			if(!document.documentElement.classList.contains('s1')) {
				excellence.querySelector('.sticky-inner').scrollLeft = 0;
				_jump(idx);
			}
		}

		const _resize = function () {
			titleL = excellenceTitle.offsetLeft;
			titleW = excellenceTitle.clientWidth;
			totalH = excellenceTitle.clientHeight;
		}
		
		_init();

		excellenceSticky = $(excellence.querySelector('.sticky-wrap')).faveSticky(_option);
		eCard.forEach(function (el,idx) {
			el.addEventListener('keyup', function (e) {
				if (e.keyCode == 9) _keyup(el,idx);
			});
		});
	}

	// excellence slide
	const slideMotion = function () {
		const arrowWrap = excellenceList.querySelector('.excellence-arrow-wrap');

		let startP = window.innerWidth/2 - eCard[0].clientWidth/2;
		let endP = window.innerWidth/2 - eCard[0].clientWidth/2;
		let downStart = false;
		let totalIdx = 0;
		let slideMove = false;
		
		const _init = function () {
			_resize();
			_this.move(startP);

			let startEvent = ['mousedown', 'touchstart'];
			let moveEvent = ['mousemove', 'touchmove'];
			let endEvent = ['mouseup', 'touchend'];
			
			startEvent.forEach(function (__this) {
				excellenceListUl.addEventListener(__this, function (e) {
					_touch.start(e);
				});
			});
			moveEvent.forEach(function (__this) {
				document.addEventListener(__this, function (e) {
					_touch.move(e);
				}, {passive: false});
			});
			endEvent.forEach(function (__this) {
				document.addEventListener(__this, function (e) {
					_touch.end(e);
				});
			});

			arrowWrap.querySelector('.prev').addEventListener('click', function (e) {
				_prev();
			});
			arrowWrap.querySelector('.next').addEventListener('click', function (e) {
				_next();
			});
			window.addEventListener('resize', function (e) {
				_resize();
			});
		}

		const _touch = {
			prevX: 0,
			prevY: 0,
			currentX: 0,
			moveX: startP,
			dragX : 0,
			endIdx :0,
			start : function (e) {
				if (!slideMove) {
					downStart = true;
					this.prevX = (e.type != 'touchstart') ? e.pageX :e.changedTouches[0].clientX;
					this.prevY = (e.type != 'touchstart') ? e.pageY :e.changedTouches[0].clientY;
				}
			},
			move : function (e) {
				if(downStart && !slideMove && document.documentElement.classList.contains('s1')) {
					this.currentX = (e.type != 'touchmove') ? e.pageX : e.changedTouches[0].clientX;
					this.currentY = (e.type != 'touchmove') ? e.pageY : e.changedTouches[0].clientY;
					
					if(!document.documentElement.classList.contains('rtl')) {
						this.dragX = Math.min(startP, this.moveX + (this.currentX-this.prevX));
						this.dragX = Math.max((-totalW+window.innerWidth-endP), this.dragX);
						
						if ((this.prevX-this.currentX) > 0) {
							this.endIdx = Math.floor(((eCard[0].clientWidth)-this.dragX) / (eCard[0].clientWidth));
						}else {
							this.endIdx = Math.floor(((window.innerWidth/4)-this.dragX) / (eCard[0].clientWidth));
						}
					}else {
						this.dragX = Math.max(-startP, this.moveX + (this.currentX-this.prevX));
						this.dragX = Math.min((totalW-window.innerWidth+endP), this.dragX);

						if ((this.prevX-this.currentX) > 0) {
							this.endIdx = Math.floor(((eCard[0].clientWidth)+this.dragX) / (eCard[0].clientWidth));
						}else {
							this.endIdx = Math.floor(((window.innerWidth/4)+this.dragX) / (eCard[0].clientWidth));
						}
					}
					if (this.currentX > this.currentY && Math.abs(this.prevY-this.currentY) <= 80) {
						e.preventDefault();
					}
					e.preventDefault();
					_this.move(this.dragX);
					
				}
			},
			end : function () {
				downStart = false;
				if (Math.abs(this.currentX) > 0) _jump(this.endIdx);

				this.prevX = 0;
				this.currentX = 0;
			}
		}

		const cardAriaHidden = function (idx) {
			eCard.forEach(function (i,index) {
				if(idx !== index) {
					i.setAttribute('aria-hidden', true);
					i.setAttribute('tabindex', -1);
					i.querySelectorAll('a').forEach(function (j) {
						j.setAttribute('aria-hidden', true);
						j.setAttribute('tabindex', -1);
					});
				}else {
					i.removeAttribute('aria-hidden');
					i.removeAttribute('tabindex');
					i.querySelectorAll('a').forEach(function (j) {
						j.removeAttribute('aria-hidden');
						j.removeAttribute('tabindex');
					});
				}

				if((!document.documentElement.classList.contains('s1'))) {
					i.removeAttribute('aria-hidden');
					i.removeAttribute('tabindex');
					i.querySelectorAll('a').forEach(function (j) {
						j.removeAttribute('aria-hidden');
						j.removeAttribute('tabindex');
					});
				}
			});
		}

		const _jump = function (idx) {
			if(!slideMove) {
				slideMove = true;

				let cardStart = eCard[idx].clientWidth*idx;
				let cardMargin;
				if(!document.documentElement.classList.contains('rtl')) {
					cardMargin = parseInt(window.getComputedStyle(eCard[eCard.length-1]).getPropertyValue('margin-left'),10)*idx;
				}else {
					cardMargin = parseInt(window.getComputedStyle(eCard[eCard.length-1]).getPropertyValue('margin-right'),10)*idx;
				}
				let cardCenter = (window.innerWidth/2) - (eCard[idx].clientWidth/2);
				
				let cardMove;
				if(!document.documentElement.classList.contains('rtl')) {
					cardMove = -cardStart - cardMargin + cardCenter;
				}else {
					cardMove = cardStart + cardMargin - cardCenter;
				}

				if(idx === 0) {
					arrowWrap.querySelector('.prev').classList.add('hide');
					if(arrowClick) {
						setTimeout(function () {
							arrowWrap.querySelector('.next').focus();
						},300);
					}
				}else {
					arrowWrap.querySelector('.prev').classList.remove('hide');
				}

				if(idx >= eCard.length-1) {
					arrowWrap.querySelector('.next').classList.add('hide');
					if(arrowClick) {
						setTimeout(function () {
							arrowWrap.querySelector('.prev').focus();
						},300);
					}
				}else {
					arrowWrap.querySelector('.next').classList.remove('hide');
				}

				let moveElement = (!document.documentElement.classList.contains('s1')) ? excellenceListUl : excellenceMobileMove;
				TweenMax.fromTo(moveElement, .5, {
					x:_touch.dragX
				},{
					x:cardMove,
					ease: Quint.easeOut,
					onComplete:function () {
						_touch.moveX = cardMove;
						_touch.dragX = cardMove;
						totalIdx = idx;
						slideMove = false;
						arrowClick = false;
						cardAriaHidden(idx);
					}
				});
			}
		}

		const _prev = function () {
			arrowClick = true;
			totalIdx = Math.max(0,totalIdx - 1);
			_jump(totalIdx);
		}
		
		const _next = function () {
			arrowClick = true;
			totalIdx = Math.min(eCard.length-1,totalIdx + 1);
			_jump(totalIdx);
		}
		let fakeDiv = document.createElement('div');
		const _resize = function () {
			startP = window.innerWidth/2 - eCard[0].clientWidth/2;
			endP = window.innerWidth/2 - eCard[0].clientWidth/2;

			if(document.documentElement.classList.contains('s1')) _jump(totalIdx);

			blankDiv.style.height = 'var(--snbh)';
			let _snbh = blankDiv.clientHeight;
			
			if ((window.innerHeight - cloneList.clientHeight-_snbh) < 0) {
				// static
				excellence.classList.add('static');
			}else {
				// sticky
				excellence.classList.remove('static');
			}
		}
		
		GALAXY.load(function () {
			_init();
		});
	}

	const move = function (_move) {
		let moveElement = (!document.documentElement.classList.contains('s1')) ? excellenceListUl : excellenceMobileMove;
		moveElement.style.transform = 'translate3d('+_move+'px,0px,0px) rotate(0.001deg)';
	}
	const resize = function () {
		totalW = 0;
		eCard.forEach(function (_this) {
			let _marginLeft;
			if(!document.documentElement.classList.contains('rtl')) {
				_marginLeft = parseInt(window.getComputedStyle(_this).getPropertyValue('margin-left'),10); 
			}else {
				_marginLeft = parseInt(window.getComputedStyle(_this).getPropertyValue('margin-right'),10); 
			}
			totalW += (_this.clientWidth+_marginLeft);
		});
		excellenceListUl.style.width = totalW + 'px';
	}
	
	return {
		init : init,
		move : move,
		resize : resize
	}
})();

excellenceMotion && excellenceMotion.init();

const ShowroomFeatures = function () {
	const _status = {
		previousHash: null,
		currentHash: null,
		device: null,
		modalOffetTop: 0,
		isOpenedModal: false,
		isOpenedTooltip: false,
		isOpenedTracker: false,
		isLoadingAssets: false,
		isReadyViewer: false,
		parent: 'showroom',
		overviewLastControl: null,
		oAccessibility: null,
		hiddenAria: {'tabindex': '-1', 'aria-hidden': 'true'},
		removeHidenAria: 'tabindex aria-hidden',
		hivelabMenu: 'see-in-360|compare',
		startHiveLab: null,
		isParentShowroom: function() {
			return _status.parent === 'showroom';
		},
		isInHivelab: function() {
			return _status.hivelabMenu.indexOf(_status.previousHash) >= 0 && _status.hivelabMenu.indexOf(_status.currentHash) >= 0;
		},
		isFromHivelab: function(tobeHash) {
			return _status.hivelabMenu.indexOf(_status.previousHash) >= 0 && _status.hivelabMenu.indexOf(tobeHash) === -1;
		},
		isHivelab: function() {
			return _status.hivelabMenu.indexOf(_status.currentHash) >= 0;
		},
		isHiveSingle: function() {
			return _status.currentHash === 'see-in-360';
		},
		indexHivelab: function() {
			if( !_status.isHivelab() ) return;
			return _status.currentHash === 'compare' ? 1 : 0;
		},
		setIsOpenTooltip: function(value) {
			this.isOpenedTooltip = value;
			this.effectOpenTooltip();
		},
		effectOpenTooltip: function() {
			if( GALAXY.sizeMode > 2 ) {
				if( m3DViewer.isOpenPopState ) {
					mTradeIn.disabled(true);
					mModal.disabledClose(true);
				} else {
					mTradeIn.disabled(false);
					mModal.disabledClose(false);
				}

				m3DViewer.enableBottomDeem(false);
				mActions.setDisabled(false);
			} else {
				if( _status.isOpenedTooltip || m3DViewer.isOpenPopState ) {
					if( m3DViewer.isOpenPopState ) {
						m3DViewer.enableBottomDeem(true);
					}
					mActions.setDisabled(true);
					mTradeIn.disabled(true);
					mModal.disabledClose(true);
					mInfoHeader.accessibillity.on();
				} else {
					mActions.setDisabled(false);
					mTradeIn.disabled(false);	
					mModal.disabledClose(false);
					m3DViewer.enableBottomDeem(false);
					mInfoHeader.accessibillity.off();
				}
			}
		},
		setIsOpenTracker: function(value) {
			this.isOpenedTracker = value;
			this.effectOpenTracker();
		},
		effectOpenTracker: function() {
			if( this.isOpenedTracker ) {
				_dom.$baseContentsArea.find('.modal_inner').scrollTop(0);
			} else {
				mActions.focusMenu();
			}
		},
		isOpenGNBMenu: function() {
			let opened = false;
			if( GALAXY.isGalaxy ) {
				opened = $('#wrap #gnb').hasClass('show') || $('#subnav .nav-dropdown .drop-menus').hasClass('open');
			} else {
				opened = $('.dotcom .gnb .gnb__menu-wrap').hasClass('open')
					|| $('.dotcom .gnb .gnb__menu-wrap').hasClass('active')
					|| $('.dotcom #content .pd-g-floating-nav .menu').hasClass('open')
					|| $('.gnb-search').css('display') === 'block'
					|| $('#layerEmptyCart').css('display') === 'block';
			}
			return opened;
		}
	}
	let _scenario = [];
	const _dom = {};

	// [init] DOM
	const _initDOM = function() {
		_dom.$hash = _dom.$modal.find('[data-hash]');
		_dom.$baseContentsArea = $('#wrap');
		if(GALAXY.isGalaxy) {
			_dom.$baseContentsArea = _dom.$baseContentsArea.find('#contents > *:not(#subnav), #footer');
		} else {
			_dom.$baseContentsArea = _dom.$baseContentsArea.find('#contents > *:not(.floating-navigation__wrap), .m_dotcom_footer, .nv-g-breadcrumb, footer');
		}
		_dom.$loadingBar = _dom.$modal.find('.load-bar');
		_dom.$targetContents = null;
		_dom.$featureContents = _dom.$modal.find('.showroom-modal-contents');
	}

	// [init]
	const _init = function(options) {
		if( options && options.parent ) {
			_status.parent = options.parent;
		}

		if( typeof(oAccessibility) !== 'undefined' ) {
			_status.oAccessibility = oAccessibility;
		}
		_status.device = $('#contents').data('model');
		if( _status.isParentShowroom() ) {
			_dom.$modal = mModal.init();

			_initDOM();
			_bindEvent();

			mStorage.initData();
			mTracker.init();
			mActions.init();
			mTradeIn.init();

			_handleHashChange();
		} else {
			_dom.$modal = options.modal;
			_initDOM();

			mStorage.initData();
			mActions.init();
		}
	}

	// events: hash change
	const _handleHashChange = function() {
		const tobeHash = window.location.hash.split('#')[1];

		if( tobeHash !== undefined && tobeHash !== _status.currentHash ) {
			mRender.hideContents();
		}

		if( tobeHash !== _status.currentHash ) {
			mHash.beforeUpdateHash();
		}
	}

	// events: binding
	const _bindEvent = function() {
		if( !_status.isParentShowroom() ) {
			return false;
		}

		window.addEventListener('hashchange', _handleHashChange, false);
	}

	const _setOverViewLastControl = function(control) {
		_status.overviewLastControl = $(control);
	}

	// [module storage]
	const mStorage = {
		initData: function() {
			_dom.$hash.each(function() {
				const $item = $(this);
				const splitHash = $item.data('hash').split('|');

				if( splitHash.length > 1 ) {
					for( let i=0; i<splitHash.length; i++ ) {
						_scenario.push({
							uid: splitHash[i],
							tagging: $item.data('tagging').split('|')[i],
							category: $item.data("category-" + splitHash[i]),
							tracker: $item.data("tracker-" + splitHash[i]),
							continueTracker: $item.data("continue-tracker-" + splitHash[i]),
							visited: false,
						})
					}
				} else {
					_scenario.push({
						uid: $item.data('hash'),
						tagging: $item.data('tagging'),
						category: $item.data('category'),
						tracker: $item.data('tracker'),
						continueTracker: $item.data('continue-tracker'),
						visited: false,
					})
				}
			});

			const __temp = [];
			_scenario.forEach(function(item) {
				const _exist = mStorage.getDataByKey(item.uid);
				__temp.push({
					uid: item.uid,
					tagging: item.tagging,
					category: item.category,
					tracker: item.tracker,
					continueTracker: item.continueTracker,
					visited: _exist !== null ? _exist.visited : false,
				});
			});

			mStorage.setAllData(__temp);
		},
		initHighlightData: function($container) {
			if( !$container ) return;

			const $hash = $container.find('[data-hash]');
			$hash.each(function() {
				const $item = $(this);
				_scenario.push({
					uid: $item.data('hash'),
					tagging: $item.data('tagging'),
					category: null,
					tracker: $item.data('tracker'),
					continueTracker: null,
					visited: null,
				})
			});
			
			const __temp = [];
			_scenario.forEach(function(item) {
				const _exist = mStorage.getDataByKey(item.uid);
				__temp.push({
					uid: item.uid,
					tagging: item.tagging,
					category: null,
					tracker: item.tracker,
					continueTracker: null,
					visited: null
				});
			});

			mStorage.setAllData(__temp);
		},
		resetData: function() {
			_scenario = [];
			mStorage.setAllData(_scenario);
		},
		getGroupByKey: function(key) {
			const data = JSON.parse(window.sessionStorage.getItem(_status.device));
			return Object.values(mStorage.utils.groupByKey(data, key));
		},
		getAllData: function() {
			let data;
			if( _status.isParentShowroom() ) {
				data = window.sessionStorage.getItem(_status.device);
			} else {
				data = window.sessionStorage.getItem(_status.parent+_status.device);
			}
			if( data === null ) {
				return null;
			}
			return JSON.parse(data);
		},
		setAllData: function(data) {
			_scenario = data;
			if( _status.isParentShowroom() ) {
				window.sessionStorage.setItem(_status.device, JSON.stringify(data));
			} else {
				window.sessionStorage.setItem(_status.parent+_status.device, JSON.stringify(data));
			}
		},
		getIndexByKey: function(key) {
			const data = mStorage.getAllData();
			let returnIndex = -1;
			const currentData = data.filter(function(item, index) {
				if( item.uid === key ) {
					returnIndex = index
					return item;
				}
			});
			return returnIndex;
		},
		getPreviewDataByKey: function(key) {
			const data = mStorage.getAllData();
			const currentIndex = mStorage.getIndexByKey(key);
			let index = currentIndex - 1;
			if( index < 0 ) {
				index = data.length - 1;
			}

			return data[index];
		},
		getNextDataByKey: function(key) {
			const data = mStorage.getAllData();
			const currentIndex = mStorage.getIndexByKey(key);
			let index = currentIndex + 1;
			if( index >= data.length ) {
				index = 0;
			}

			return data[index];
		},
		getDataByKey: function(key) {
			const data = mStorage.getAllData();
			if( data !== null ) {
				const result = data.filter(function(item) {
					return item.uid === key;
				});

				if( result.length === 0 ) {
					return null;
				}

				return result[0];
			} else {
				return null;
			}
		},
		setDataByKey: function(key, visited) {
			let allData = mStorage.getAllData();
			let currentIndex = -1;
			const currentData = allData.filter(function(item, index) {
				if( item.uid === key ) {
					currentIndex = index
					return item;
				}
			});

			if( currentData.length === 0 ) {
				return false;
			}

			const updateItem = {
				uid: currentData[0].uid,
				tagging: currentData[0].tagging,
				category: currentData[0].category,
				tracker: currentData[0].tracker,
				continueTracker: currentData[0].continueTracker,
				visited: visited,
			}
			allData[currentIndex] = updateItem;
			mStorage.setAllData(allData);
		},
		getVisitedData: function() {
			const data = mStorage.getAllData();
			if( data === null ) return [];
			return data.filter(function(item) {
				return item.visited === true;
			});
		},
		getRemainedData: function() {
			const data = mStorage.getAllData();
			if( data === null ) return [];
			return data.filter(function(item) {
				return item.visited === false;
			});
		},
		utils: {
			groupByKey: function(array, key) {
				return array.reduce(function(hash, obj) {
					hash[obj[key]] = hash[obj[key]] || [];
					hash[obj[key]].push(obj);
					return hash;
				}, {});
			}
		}
	}

	// [modlue hash]
	const mHash = {
		beforeUpdateHash: function() {
			if( !_status.isParentShowroom() ) {
				return false;
			}

			const tobeHash = window.location.hash.split('#')[1];
			if( tobeHash === 'ar' ) {
				return false;
			}

			if( tobeHash === undefined ) {
				if( _status.isOpenedModal ) {
					mRender.hideModal();
				}
				mHash.updateHash('');
				return false;
			}

			_status.previousHash = _status.currentHash ? _status.currentHash : null;

			const tobeScenario = _scenario.filter(function(item) {
				return item.uid === tobeHash;
			});

			if( tobeScenario.length > 0 ) {
				if( _status.isFromHivelab(tobeHash) ) {
					/// 360 exit callback
					m3DViewer.exit(function() {
						mHash.updateHash(tobeHash);
					})
				} else {
					mHash.updateHash(tobeHash);
				}

			} else {
				mRender.hideModal();
				mHash.updateHash('');
			}
		},
		updateHash: function(hash) {
			if( _status.isParentShowroom() ) {
				window.location.hash = hash;
			}
			_status.currentHash = hash;

			if( _status.isHivelab() && _status.startHiveLab === null ) {
				_status.startHiveLab = _status.currentHash;
			}

			mRender.render();
		}
	}

	// [render]
	const mRender = {
		$infoHeader: null,
		render: function() {
			this.showModal();
			if( !_status.isOpenedModal ) { return false; }
			if( _status.isHivelab() ) { !m3DViewer.initial && m3DViewer.init(); }
			mVideo.init(_status.currentHash);
		},
		renderContents: function() {
			if( _status.currentHash === '' ) return false;
			_dom.$targetContents = _dom.$modal.find('article[data-hash*=' + _status.currentHash + ']');
			mActions.render();
			if( _status.isHivelab() ) { m3DViewer.render(); }
			this.accessibillity.on();
			setTimeout(mRender.showContents, 150);
		},
		showContents: function() {
			if( _dom.$targetContents ) {
				_dom.$targetContents.css('display', 'block').stop().__animate({
					opacity: 1
				}, { duration: 500, onComplete: function(){
					_dom.$targetContents.addClass('show-feature');
				} });
				_dom.$targetContents.attr('data-current', _status.currentHash);
				_dom.$targetContents.trigger('visible');
				mVideo.render();
			}

			mInfoHeader.init();
			mActions.show();

			if( _status.isParentShowroom() ) {
				mModal.updateScrollButtonTagging();
				mModal.handleResize();
			}
			if( _status.isParentShowroom() ) {
				mInfoHeader.show();
			} else {
				if( GALAXY.sizeMode > 2 ) {
					mInfoHeader.show();
				}
			}

			if( _status.isHivelab() ) { m3DViewer.show(); }
			mStorage.setDataByKey(_status.currentHash, true);
			mTracker.render();
		},
		hideContents: function() {
			mVideo.stop();
			mActions.hide();
			mInfoHeader.hide();
			mTracker.hide();

			if( _status.currentHash ) {
				const $targetPrevContents = _dom.$modal.find('article[data-hash*=' + _status.currentHash + ']');
				if( $targetPrevContents ) {
					$targetPrevContents.stop().__animate({
						opacity: 0
					}, { duration: 500, onComplete: function(){
						$targetPrevContents.css('display', 'none').removeClass('show-feature');
					} });
					$targetPrevContents.attr('data-current', '');
				}
			}
		},
		removeContents: function() {
			this.hideContents();

			if( _dom.$targetContents !== null  ) {
				_dom.$targetContents.removeAttr('style').removeClass('show-feature');
				_dom.$targetContents.attr('data-current', '');
			}
		},
		showModal: function() {
			if( !_status.isParentShowroom() || _status.isOpenedModal || _status.currentHash === '' ) {
				return false;
			}

			mModal.show();
		},
		hideModal: function() {
			if( !_status.isParentShowroom() ) {
				return false;
			}
			setTimeout(function() {
				mRender.removeContents();
				mModal.hide();
			}, 0);
		},
		renderLoading: function() {
			if( !_dom.$loadingBar ) {
				return false;
			}

			if( _status.isLoadingAssets ) {
                _dom.$loadingBar.find('.load-img img').attr('alt', _dom.$loadingBar.find('.load-img').data('alt') );
                _dom.$loadingBar.find('span').text('');
				_dom.$loadingBar.removeClass('hide-load-bar').removeAttr(_status.removeHidenAria);
            } else {
                _dom.$loadingBar.find('.load-img img').attr('alt', _dom.$loadingBar.find('.load-img').data('alt') );
                _dom.$loadingBar.find('span').text(_dom.$loadingBar.data('load-txt'));
				setTimeout(function () {
					_dom.$loadingBar.addClass('hide-load-bar').attr(_status.hiddenAria);
				},500);
            }			
		},
		accessibillity: {
			on: function() {
				// disclaimer
				if( _dom.$targetContents && _dom.$targetContents.find('.header-disclaimer').length ) {
					const $disclaimer = _dom.$targetContents.find('.header-disclaimer');
					const countDisclaimer = $disclaimer.find('.c_desc-type1').length;
					if( countDisclaimer > 1 ) {
						$disclaimer.attr('role', 'list');
						$disclaimer.find('.c_desc-type1').each( function() {
							const $this = $(this);
							$this.attr('role', 'listitem');
						});
					}
				}
			},
		}
	}

	// [module Video]
	const mVideo = {
		$targetContents: null,
		$video: null,
		$btnPlay: null,
		sizeVideo: null,
		playState: 'stop',
		pausedInfo: false,
		initial: false,
		init: function(hash) {
			this.$targetContents = _dom.$modal.find('article[data-hash*=' + hash + ']');
			this.loadAssets();
			GALAXY.resize(this.handleResize, true);
		},
		loadAssets: function() {
			_status.isLoadingAssets = true;
			mRender.renderLoading();

			let $lazyLoadAssets = this.$targetContents.find('.none-lazy-load');
			let total = $lazyLoadAssets.length;
			let loadNum = 0;

			$lazyLoadAssets.find('img').each(function( i, image ) {
				let src = GALAXY.setMediaBaseURL( GALAXY.getImageSources($(image))[GALAXY.sizeMode] );
				$(this).attr('src', src);
				$(this).one('load.loadImages error.loadImages', function () {
					if( loadNum >= total-1 ) {
						mVideo.afterLoad();
					}
					loadNum += 1;
					$(this).off('load.loadImages error.loadImages');
				});
			});

			$lazyLoadAssets.each(function () {
				const $video = $(this);
				if( $video.hasClass('video') && !$video.data('loaded') ) {
					$video.data('loaded', true);

					GALAXY.setNewVideoControl($(this), $(this).parents('article'));
				}
			});

			if ( !total ) {
				mVideo.afterLoad();
			}
		},
		afterLoad: function() {
			this.$video = this.$targetContents.find('video');
			this.$btnPlay = this.$targetContents.find('.btn_click-video');
			this.$video.on('loadedmetadata', function() {
				mVideo.sizeVideo = {
					height: this.videoHeight,
					width: this.videoWidth
				}
			});
			_status.isLoadingAssets = false;
			mRender.renderLoading();
			mRender.renderContents();
			this.initial = true;
		},
		render: function() {
			const _ = this;
			if( !_.initial ) return false;
			_.handleVideoChange();

			mVideo.readyPlay();

			_.$video.off('pause.video').on('pause.video', function(event) {
				_.setPlayState('pause');
			})
			_.$video.off('play.video').on('play.video', function(event) {
				_.setPlayState('playing');
			})
			_.$video.off('timeupdate.feature').on('timeupdate.feature', function () {
				_.$btnPlay.removeClass('btn-replay');
			});
			_.$video.off('ended.feature').on('ended.feature', function () {
				_.$btnPlay.addClass('btn-startover');
				_.$btnPlay.find('span').text(_.$btnPlay.data('replay-title'));
				_.setPlayState('stop');
			});
			_.$targetContents.find('.m_video-wrap .btn_click-video').off('click.feature-control click.feature-control-tracking').on('click.feature-control', function (e) {
				e.preventDefault();

				const $this = $(this);
				if( $this.hasClass('btn-startover') ) {
					_.$video[0].currentTime = 0;
					_.$video[0].play();
					_.$btnPlay.removeClass('btn-startover');
					_.$btnPlay.find('span').text(_.$btnPlay.data('pause-title'));
				}
			}).on('click.feature-control-tracking', GALAXY.tracking);

			setTimeout(_.handleResize, 100);
			_.$video.on('loadedmetadata', function() {
				_.sizeVideo = {
					height: this.videoHeight,
					width: this.videoWidth
				}
				setTimeout(_.resizeAspectRatio, 100);
			});
		},
		setPlayState: function(state) {
			const _ = this;
			_.playState = state;
		},
		pause: function() {
			const _ = this;
			if( !_.initial ) return false;

			if( _.playState === 'playing' ) {
				_.$btnPlay.trigger('click');
				_.pausedInfo = true;
			}
		},
		resume: function() {
			const _ = this;
			if( !_.initial ) return false;

			if( _.pausedInfo && _.playState === 'pause' ) {
				_.$btnPlay.trigger('click');
				_.pausedInfo = false;
			}
		},
		stop: function() {
			const _ = this;
			if( !_.initial ) return false;

			if( _.playState === 'playing' ) {
				_.$btnPlay.trigger('click');
			}
			if( _.$video.length > 0 ) {
				_.$video.attr('class', 'ready');
				_.$video[0].currentTime = 0;
			}
			_.pausedInfo = false;
			_.setPlayState('stop');
		},
		resetPlay: function() {
			const _ = this;
			if( !_.initial ) return false;

			_.stop();
			_.$btnPlay.trigger('click');
		},
		play: function() {
			const _ = this;
			if( !_.initial ) return false;

			if( _.playState !== 'playing' ) {
				_.$btnPlay.trigger('click');
			}
		},
		readyPlay: function() {
			const _ = this;
			if( !_.initial ) return false;

			if( _.$video.hasClass('ready') ) {
				setTimeout(function () {
					if( _status.isParentShowroom() ) {
						if( GALAXY.sizeMode > 2 ) {
							mVideo.play();
						}
					} else {
						mVideo.play();
					}
				}, 1000);
			} else {
				_.$video.one('canplay.video', function () {
					setTimeout(function () {
						if( _status.isParentShowroom() ) {
							if( GALAXY.sizeMode > 2 ) {
								mVideo.play();
							}
						} else {
							mVideo.play();
						}
					}, 1000);
				});
			}
		},
		handleVideoChange: function() {
			const _ = this;
			_dom.$targetContents.trigger('video-change');
			const $cover = _dom.$targetContents.find('.hide-bg');
			const coverUrl = $cover.attr('data-bg');
			if( coverUrl !== undefined ) {
				$cover.css({'background-image': 'url('+ coverUrl +')'});
			}
		},
		resizeAspectRatio: function() {
			const _ = mVideo;
			if( !_.initial ) { return; }
			if( !_.sizeVideo ) { return; }
			if( _dom.$featureContents.css('display') === 'none' ) { return; }

			if( GALAXY.prevSizeMode !== 0 && GALAXY.sizeMode !== GALAXY.prevSizeMode ) {
				_.stop();
			}
			
			const $wrapper = _.$targetContents.find('.m_video-wrap');
			const $video = $wrapper.find('video');
			const containerSize = {
				height: $(window).height() > $wrapper.height() ? $wrapper.height() : $(window).height(),
				width: $(window).width() > $wrapper.width() ? $wrapper.width() : $(window).width()
			};

			let updatedVideoSize = {
				height: 0,
				width: 0
			}

			if( $video[0] ) {
				_.sizeVideo = {
					height: $video[0].videoHeight,
					width: $video[0].videoWidth
				}
			}

			let ratio = [containerSize.width / _.sizeVideo.width, containerSize.height / _.sizeVideo.height];
			ratio = Math.min(ratio[0], ratio[1]);

			updatedVideoSize.height = parseInt(_.sizeVideo.height * ratio, 10);
			updatedVideoSize.width = parseInt(_.sizeVideo.width * ratio, 10);

			updatedVideoSize.height += updatedVideoSize.height % 2 === 1 ? 1 : 0;
			updatedVideoSize.width += updatedVideoSize.width % 2 === 1 ? 1 : 0;

			$wrapper.find('figure.video').css({
				height: updatedVideoSize.height + "px",
				width: updatedVideoSize.width + "px",
			})
		},
		handleResize: function() {
			const _ = mVideo;
			if (GALAXY.sizeMode != GALAXY.prevSizeMode) {
				_.handleVideoChange();
			}
			_.resizeAspectRatio();
		}
	}

	// [module info header]
	const mInfoHeader = {
		$infoHeader: null,
		$btnClose: null,
		$btnPlay: null,
		$deemed: null,
		$scrollShadowContainer: null,
		$scrollContainer: null,
		initial: false,
		init: function() {
			let queryString = '.f_header-feature';
			if( _status.isHivelab() ) {
				queryString += '.' + _status.currentHash;
			}
			this.$infoHeader = _dom.$targetContents.find(queryString);
			this.$deemed = _dom.$targetContents.find('.deemed');
			this.$btnClose = this.$infoHeader.find('.btn-info-close');
			this.$scrollShadowContainer = this.$infoHeader.find('.scroll-shadow-container');
			this.setInfoHeaderMaxHeight();
			this.$scrollContainer = this.$scrollShadowContainer.find('.scroll');

			this.$deemed.on('click', this.handleClickBG);
			this.$btnClose.off('click.info-close').on('click.info-close', this.handleClickClose);

			this.$btnPlay = this.$infoHeader.find('.btn-tap');
			this.$btnPlay.off('click.tap-play').on('click.tap-play', this.handleClickPlay);

			GALAXY.resize(this.handleResize, true);
			this.handleResize();
			this.initital = true;
		},
		show: function() {
			if( !this.initital ) return;
			_status.setIsOpenTooltip(true);

			this.$infoHeader.closest('.f_container').addClass('show-header');
			this.setInfoHeaderMaxHeight();
			this.$infoHeader.addClass('show-info-header');

			GALAXY.setTransitionEndEvent(this.$infoHeader, mInfoHeader.afterShow);
		},
		afterShow: function() {
			const _ = mInfoHeader;
			if( GALAXY.sizeMode <= 2 ) {
				mInfoHeader.$btnClose.focus();
			}
			else {
				if( _status.isParentShowroom() ) { mModal.focusClose(); }
			}

			_.handleResize();
		},
		hide: function() {
			if( !this.initital ) return;

			this.$infoHeader.closest('.f_container').removeClass('show-header');
			_dom.$featureContents.find('.f_header-feature.show-info-header').removeClass('show-info-header');
			this.afterHide();
		},
		afterHide: function() {
			const _ = mInfoHeader;
			_status.setIsOpenTooltip(false);
			_.$scrollContainer.scrollTop(0);
			_.$scrollContainer.off('scroll.info');
			mActions.focusInfo();
		},
		setInfoHeaderMaxHeight: function() {
			const _ = mInfoHeader;
			const contentsHeight = _dom.$featureContents.height();
			let ratio = 0.40;
			if( GALAXY.sizeMode === 2 ) { ratio = 0.45; }
			if( GALAXY.sizeMode === 3 ) { ratio = 0.75; }
			if( GALAXY.sizeMode === 4 ) { ratio = 0.7; }
				
			const scrollHeight = _.$scrollShadowContainer.find('.scroll').prop('scrollHeight');
			let resultHeight = parseInt(contentsHeight*ratio, 10);
			_.$scrollShadowContainer.css({
				'max-height': resultHeight + "px",
				'height': 'auto'
			});

			if( $('html.ie').length && scrollHeight >= resultHeight ) {
				_.$scrollShadowContainer.css({
					'height': scrollHeight + "px",
				});
			}
		},
		accessibillity: {
			on: function() {
				let findString = '.f_video-feature';
				findString += !m3DViewer.isOpenPopState ? ', .f_3dviewer-container' : "";
				const $feature = _dom.$targetContents.find(findString);
				_status.oAccessibility && _status.oAccessibility.on($feature);

				$('body').off('keydown.closeInfoHeader').on('keydown.closeInfoHeader', function(e) {
					if( !_status.isOpenGNBMenu() && _status.isOpenedModal && _status.isOpenedTooltip && (e.key == 'Escape' || e.keyCode == 27)	) {
						mInfoHeader.handleClickClose();
					};
				});
			},
			off: function() {
				let findString = '.f_video-feature';
				findString += !m3DViewer.isOpenPopState ? ', .f_3dviewer-container' : "";
				const $feature = _dom.$targetContents.find(findString);
				_status.oAccessibility && _status.oAccessibility.off($feature);

				$('body').off('keydown.closeInfoHeader');
			}
		},
		handleClickBG: function() {
			mInfoHeader.hide();
			mVideo.resume();
			if( _status.isHivelab() ) {
				m3DViewer.continueIntroPose();
			}
		},
		handleClickClose: function() {
			mInfoHeader.hide();
			mVideo.resume();
			if( _status.isHivelab() ) {
				m3DViewer.continueIntroPose();
			}
		},
		handleClickPlay: function() {
			mInfoHeader.hide();
			mVideo.resetPlay();
			if( _status.isHivelab() ) {
				m3DViewer.continueIntroPose();
			}
		},
		handleScrollContents: function(e) {
			const _ = mInfoHeader;
			if( mInfoHeader.$scrollContainer.scrollTop() > 0 ) {
				_.$scrollShadowContainer.addClass('scrolling');
			} else {
				_.$scrollShadowContainer.removeClass('scrolling');
			}
		},
		handleResize: function() {
			const _ = mInfoHeader;
			if( !_.initital ) return;

			_.setInfoHeaderMaxHeight();

			const $container = _.$scrollContainer;
			if( $container.prop('scrollHeight') > $container.prop('clientHeight') ) {
				$container.attr('tabindex', 0);
			} else {
				$container.removeAttr('tabindex');	
			}

			$container.off('scroll.info').on('scroll.info', _.handleScrollContents);
			_.handleScrollContents();

			if( GALAXY.sizeMode > 2 ) { _.show(); }
			_status.effectOpenTooltip();
		},
	}

	// [modlue Journey Tracker]
	const mTracker = {
		initital: false,
		$trackerContainer: null,
		$btnClose: null,
		$btnBuyContainer: null,
		$btnShortcut: null,
		init: function() {
			this.$trackerContainer = $('.journey-tracker-contents');
			this.$btnClose = this.$trackerContainer.find('.btn-close');
			this.$btnClose.on('click.tracker-close', mTracker.handleClickClose);
			this.$btnShortcut = this.$trackerContainer.find('.btn-shortcut');
			this.$btnBuyContainer = this.$trackerContainer.find('.buy-container');
			this.$upgrading = this.$trackerContainer.find('.tracker-card.upgrading');
			const $upgradingItems = this.$upgrading.find('.tracker-card-list > li');
			if( $upgradingItems.length === 0 ) {
				this.$upgrading.attr(_status.hiddenAria).css('visibility', 'hidden');
			}
			this.initital = true;
		},
		render: function() {
			const _ = this;
			if( !_.initital ) return false;

			const remained = mStorage.getRemainedData();
			if( remained.length === 0 ) {
				_.$btnShortcut.addClass('hide');
				_.$btnBuyContainer.css('display', 'block');
			} else {
				const remainItem = remained[0];
				_.$btnShortcut.attr('href', '#' + remainItem.uid);
				_.$btnShortcut.attr('title', remainItem.tracker);

				let shortcutOmniture = _.$btnShortcut.data('omni');
				let shortcutOmni = shortcutOmniture.replace('{device}', _status.device);
				shortcutOmni = shortcutOmni.replace('{target}', remainItem.tagging);
				_.$btnShortcut.attr('data-omni', shortcutOmni).attr('ga-la', shortcutOmni);

				_.$btnShortcut.removeClass('hide');
				_.$btnShortcut.off('click.nav click.nav-tracking').on('click.nav', mActions.handleClickNavigation).on('click.nav-tracking', GALAXY.tracking);
				_.$btnBuyContainer.css('display', 'none');
			}

			const grouped = mStorage.getGroupByKey('category');
			grouped.forEach(function(category, index) {
				const $listContainer = _.$trackerContainer.find('#tracker-category-'+index);
				let originOmniture = $listContainer.data('omni');
				let htmlListTracker = '';
				
				category.forEach(function(item) {
					let itemOmni = originOmniture.replace('{device}', _status.device);
					itemOmni = itemOmni.replace('{current}', _status.currentHash);
					itemOmni = itemOmni.replace('{target}', item.tagging);
					const attrTitle = item.visited ? "title='" + _.$trackerContainer.data('checked-title') + "'" : "";
					const currentMenu = (item.uid === _status.currentHash);
